third quarter ended </div><div id="a211" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:439.4px;">November 2, 2019.<div style="display:inline-block;width:9.07px">&#160;</div>Sales for the third 2, 2019.<div style="display:inline-block;width:13.44px">&#160;</div>The Company&#8217;s same-store sales </div><div id="a279" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:494.6px;">for the quarter decreased 23% to the same period last year. </div><div id="a301" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:530.3px;">As previously announced, Cato closed all stores due to the COVID-19 pandemic beginning March 19, </div><div id="a333" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:557.8px;">2020.<div style="display:inline-block;width:9.11px">&#160;</div>On May 1, 2020, the Company began reopening stores in a phased approach, with limited </div><div id="a365" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:585.5px;">operating hours, consistent with local health and safety guidelines and regulations.<div style="display:inline-block;width:9.13px">&#160;</div>As of June 15, </div><div id="a395" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:613px;">2020, all stores had reopened. </div><div id="a405" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:648.7px;">For the nine months ended October 31, 2020, the Company reported a net loss of $39.2 million or </div><div id="a441" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:676.2px;">($1.64) per diluted share, compared to net income of $39.1 million or $1.59 per diluted share for the </div><div id="a477" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:703.9px;">nine months ended November 2, 2019.<div million, down 34% to sales of $627.8 million for the nine months ended November 2, 2019.<div style="display:inline-block;width:4.78px">&#160;</div></div><div id="a544" 35.8% versus 31.2% last year primarily due to the </div><div id="a1151" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:482px;">effects of deleveraging and impairment charges of $7.6 million, partially offset by company-wide </div><div id="a1180" style="position:absolute;font-size:16px;left:48px;top:509.5px;">expense reductions and the reduction of incentive compensation.<div
